interface ModalComponentProps {
    component: ModalValueProps,
    props: object
}

export const ModalRoot = () => (
    <ModalConsumer>
        {({ modals, hideModal }: ModalContextProps) => {
            return (
                Object
                    .entries(modals)
                    .map(
                        ([key, { component: Component, props }]: [string, ModalComponentProps]
                    ) => (
                        <Component {...props} key={key} hideModal={() => hideModal(key)} />
                ))
            )
        }}
    </ModalConsumer>
)

import React from 'react'
import { ModalConsumer } from './ModalContext'
import { ModalContextProps, ModalProps } from './types'

interface ModalComponentProps {
    component: React.FC<ModalProps>,
    props: object
}

export const ModalRoot = () => (
    <ModalConsumer>
        {({ modals, hideModal }: ModalContextProps) => {
            return (
                Object
                    .entries(modals)
                    .map(
                        ([key, { component: Component, props }]: [string, ModalComponentProps]
                    ) => (
                        <Component {...props} key={key} hideModal={() => hideModal(key)} />
                ))
            )
        }}
    </ModalConsumer>
)

14:26
Sander üï∂
I did improvment with user experience, but here is the case, when formik is not working well with dynamic fields.

To allow formik update initialSatem, need turn "enableReinitialize" to true and formik will check diff, if values in "initialSate" changed,
formik fill update state, but then filled inputs will be lost,
we need to get our current state and pass it back to initialState.

We update initialState, because formik need to know about new fields to show the errors.

To fix this in the future, I see two solutions:

each component field will generate "initial state" only for one field, when a component will be loaded the first time,
and no need to generate initialState manually every time, should work automatically.
create "context-api" wrapper for formik, to share "data".
